    <h2>Home</h2>

    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <h3>An Integrated Approach</h3> 
      <p>The UC Riverside Office of Strategic Communications is responsible for creating integrated programs that publicize and support the university’s mission of teaching, research and service to audiences through first-person communication, programs and publications.</p> 
      <div id="box"> 
       <ul id="ul_puzzle"> 
        <li><a id="a_osc" title="Office of Strategic Communications" href="#tab_osc"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_cds" title="Creative Design Services" href="#tab_cds"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_marketing" title="Marketing" href="#tab_marketing"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_media" title="Media Relations" href="#tab_media"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_video" title="Video Production" href="#tab_video"> </a></li> 
        <li><a id="a_web" title="Web Development" href="#tab_web"> </a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <div id="tab_osc"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/osc_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">How can Strategic Communications Help You?</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><img id="big_puzzle" class="img_L_borderless_close" src="/images/box/big_puzzle.png" alt=" " width="177" height="161" /><strong>The departments within</strong> the Office of Strategic Communications work together to promote you and your university. <img id="yellow_puzzle" class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/yellow_puzzle.png" alt=" " width="123" height="99" />Browse the tabs to learn what we do and how we do it.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_cds"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/cds_ttl.gif" alt="" width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Creative Design Services</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong><img id="cds_brochure" class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/cds_brochure.png" alt=" " width="164" height="167" />From conception to delivery</strong>, UCR’s award-winning in-house design team help colleges and departments produce communication projects that tell your story to the world.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/">Visit the Creative Design Services site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_marketing"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/marketing_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Marketing</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong>From advertising to publications</strong>, creative development to market research, the Marketing team is responsible for developing and implementing integrated marketing strategies that enhance the university’s image and reputation.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://marketing.ucr.edu/">Visit the Marketing site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_media"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/media_ttl.gif" alt="" width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Media Relations</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong>The Media Relations team</strong> communicates with media around the world to spread the news about what is happening at UC Riverside. They are also responsible for several publications, including <cite>UCR Magazine</cite> and <cite>Inside UCR</cite>.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/">Visit the Media Relations site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_video"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/video_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Video Production</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/video_image.png" alt=" " width="199" height="146" />UCR’s primary source for</strong> original video and television programming. Its facilities have full post-production capabilities and are a vast resource of the campus and the Inland Southern California community.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://videoproduction.ucr.edu/">Visit the Video Production site</a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div id="tab_web"> 
        <img class="border_image_top" src="/images/box/web_ttl.gif" alt=" " width="504" height="72" /> 
        <h3 class="accessibility">Web Development</h3> 
        <h4 class="accessibility">A Diverse Set of Marketing and Promotional Services for UC Riverside</h4> 
        <p><strong><img class="img_R_borderless_close" src="/images/box/web_dev_image.png" alt=" " width="157" height="163" />The Web Development team</strong> is responsible for the design and upkeep of the award-winning UCR “Umbrella” website as well as oversight of the university’s overall online presence.</p> 
        <p><a class="standout2" href="http://webdevelopment.ucr.edu/">Visit the Web Development site</a></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="divided3"> 
       <div class="column3"> 
        <h3><img id="ucr_mag" src="/images/ucr_mag_ttl.png" alt="UCR Magazine: Quarterly Publication" width="187" height="140" /></h3> 
        <p>Read the <a href="http://magazine.ucr.edu/">latest issue of our campus magazine</a>.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="column3"> 
        <h3><img id="inside_ucr" src="/images/inside_ucr_ttl.png" alt="Inside UCR: Bi-Monthly Publication" width="187" height="140" /></h3> 
        <p>See the <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/inside-ucr">latest on-campus news</a> with our in-house newspaper.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="column3R"> 
        <h3><img id="ucr_youtube" src="/images/ucr_youtube_ttl.png" alt="UCR on YouTube" width="186" height="124" /></h3> 
        <p>View the <a class="external" title="external site: YouTube" href="http://www.youtube.com/ucriverside">UC Riverside channel</a> on YouTube.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="clear"></div> 
      </div> 
      <h3><img src="/images/media_training_ttl.gif" alt="Media Training" width="167" height="38" /></h3> 
      <p>Want some <a href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/training.html">pointers about upcoming interviews</a> with the media? Our public information officers are here to help.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/portrait_scheduler_ttl.png" alt="Portrait Scheduler" width="209" height="35" /></h3> 
      <p>The Video Production Unit can take professional-quality head shots of UCR faculty for both university and personal use. <a href="/cgi-bin/photo/schedule.cgi">Visit the Portrait Scheduler</a> to schedule an appointment.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/identity_standards_manual_ttl.gif" alt="Identity Standars Manual" width="263" height="38" /></h3> 
      <p>The <a href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/ism/">Identity Standards Manual</a> will ensure that your communications materials adhere to the campus’ brand standards to facilitate smooth project development.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/ucr_web_toolbox_ttl.gif" alt="UCR Web Toolbox" width="182" height="45" /></h3> 
      <p>A list of resources that can help you build and maintain a great website.</p> 
      <h3 class="section"><img src="/images/ibooks_guide_ttle.png" alt="UCR iBooks Guide" width="190" height="45" /></h3> 
      <p>Want to view your favorite UCR Publications on your iPad? Check out our <a href="/ibooks/">ibooks guide</a> to learn how.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

     <h2 class="intro big"> Transfers</h2> 
     <img class="centerImg header" alt="" width="582" height="247" src="/Images/header_transfer.jpg" /> 
     <div class="grid_10 prefix_1 suffix_1 alpha omega"> 
      <div class="clearfix centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="verd intro grey" style="margin-bottom: 0;"> Guaranteed admission, financial aid, how to apply<br /> and just being reassured that you belong at UCR. </h3> 
       <a class="rightArrowCTA xlarge" href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_transfer.pdf">Print a Transfer Checklist</a> 
      </div> 
      <hr class="style1" style="margin-bottom: 30px;" /> 
      <div class="genericBody version2 verd clearfix"> 
       <div class="grid_5 alpha"> 
        <h4> How to Transfer </h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>See UCR’s&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/pathsAdmissions#transferStudents">transfer admission and major requirements.</a></li> 
         <li>Use the <a href="http://admission.universityofcalifornia.edu/transfer/transfer-admission-planner/index.html">Transfer Admission Planner (TAP)</a> to plan and track your course work.</li> 
         <li>Learn about our&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR/ourGuarantee#transferStudents">Transfer Admission Guarantee (TAG)</a> program.</li> 
         <li>Explore <a href="http://www.assist.org/web-assist/welcome.html">ASSIST</a> to <a href="http://web1.assist.org/web-assist/help/help-transferable_courses.html">find out if your courses will transfer</a> and <a href="http://www2.assist.org/exploring-majors/findMajorListByInstitutionAbbrev.do?abbrev=UCR">see prerequisites for your intended major</a>.&nbsp;&nbsp; </li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4> How You Can Afford It</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Find out how&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/PayingForCollege/costEstimator">how affordable</a>&nbsp;it is to attend UCR.</li> 
         <li>Discover the&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/PayingForCollege/financialAidScholarships">many ways</a>&nbsp;UCR makes college possible, regardless of financial challenges.</li> 
         <li>See if you qualify for our <a href="http://alumni.ucr.edu/Page.aspx?pid=357">Re-entry Scholarship</a>.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4> How You Will Fit In</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Meet&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/WhyUCR/ourStudents">our students.</a></li> 
         <li>Plug right in to&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/CampusLife">campus life.</a></li> 
         <li>Live in our&nbsp;<a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/liveUCR/special-interest-housing.aspx">Transfer Student Theme Hall</a>, <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/housing-options/campus-apartments/default.aspx">campus apartments</a> or <a href="http://housing.ucr.edu/housing-options/family-student-housing.aspx">family housing</a>.</li> 
         <li>Come to <a href="http://highlanderday.ucr.edu/">Highlander Day.</a></li> 
         <li>Join transfer student organizations such as the <a href="http://highlanderlink.ucr.edu/organization/tausigma">Tau Sigma National Honor Society</a>, <a href="http://highlanderlink.ucr.edu/organization/tsa">Transfer Student Association</a> and the <a href="http://highlanderlink.ucr.edu/organization/puenteconnection">Puente Connection</a> club (once enrolled).</li> 
         <li>Schedule&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/VisitUCR/tourOptions">a campus tour</a>&nbsp;or take a <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/VisitUCR/virtualTours">virtual tour</a>&nbsp;right now.</li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <div class="grid_5 omega"> 
        <h4> How to Apply</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>See a&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Apply">step-by-step guide</a>&nbsp;to the application process.</li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_transfer.pdf">Print a Transfer Checklist</a> for a detailed timeline.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4> How We Support You</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Academics/supportServices">See support services</a> for military, those with special needs and more.</li> 
         <li>Discover <a href="/Academics/transferprep">unique transfer programs</a> including the Smart Start Transfer Academy and Puente Connection.</li> 
         <li>Find out how we boost your <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/CampusLife/safetyWellness">health and wellness</a>. </li> 
         <li>Discover our unique <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/students/ethnic_gender.html">Ethnic &amp; Gender Programs.</a></li> 
         <li>Learn about free tutoring at the <a href="http://arc.ucr.edu/">Academic Resource Center.</a></li> 
         <li>Explore&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Academics/honorsPrograms">honors opportunities</a>&nbsp;for transfer students.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4> How to Stay Connected</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Like us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ucradmissions" target="_blank">Facebook</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow us on <a href="https://twitter.com/ucradmissions" target="_blank">Twitter</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow us on <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/" target="_blank">Tumblr</a>.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4> How to Get Help</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="mailto:transfer@ucr.edu">Email a transfer admissions counselor.</a></li> 
         <li>See answers to&nbsp;<a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Home/FAQ">frequently asked questions.</a></li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>

    Y.later(10, this, function() {// Temporary hack for triggering UH animation for Save It Later
                Y.Global.detach('saveforlater|*');
                Y.Global.on('saveforlater|saveforlater:newsaved', function()
                {
                    var tabIcon = Y.one('#yucsHead .yucs-avatar.yucs-menu_anchor'),
                        sflIcon = tabIcon && tabIcon.one('.sfl-icon');

                    if (tabIcon && !sflIcon)
                    {
                        var repeats = 0, callback = null;
                        
                        sflIcon = Y.Node.create('<i class="icon-y-xsmall selected sfl-icon"></i>');
                        sflIcon.setStyles({
                            'opacity': 0,
                            'boxShadow': '0px 0px 20px #400090'
                        });
                        tabIcon.prepend(sflIcon);

                        callback = function ()
                        {
                            sflIcon.transition({
                                duration: 0.6,
                                opacity: (repeats + 1) % 2
                            });
                            repeats++;
                            if (repeats < 4)
                                Y.later(600, this, callback); // the animation duration for each is 600ms
                            else
                                Y.later(600, this, function () {sflIcon.remove();});
                        };
                        Y.later(10, this, callback);
                    }
                });});

                        var cnt = (rendered_pos_ids && rendered_pos_ids.length) || 0,   
                            pos_id, pos_list = ['LREC','LREC2', 'LREC3'],
                            adContainer, adModule;

                        for(var k in pos_list){ 
                            pos_id = pos_list[k];
                            adModule = Y.one('.yog-rp #yom-ad-' + pos_id);
                            if(!adModule) {

                                     && adContainer.getComputedStyle('height') === '1px')
                                 || adContainer.getComputedStyle('width') === '0px'

                        if (!cnt) {
                            return;

                        });     
                        Y.log('fetch ad success: ' + rendered_pos_ids.join(', '), 'info', 'darla');

                    DARLA_CONFIG.onFailure = function (eventId) {
                        var positions = null;
                        try {
                            positions = DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].ps.split(',');
                        } catch (e) {}

                        Y.Global.fire('darla:failure', {
                            positions: positions
                        });
                        Y.log('fetch ad failure ' + eventId + (positions ? (': ' + positions.join(', ')) : ''), 'warn', 'darla');
                    };

                    DARLA_CONFIG.onFinishParse = function(eventId, result) {
                        var noads = [], ps = result.ps(),
                            i, l, position, posObj, mutexPos, posName, container, display,
                            re = /([A-Z0-9]+)(-[0-9]+)*/;
                    
                        for (i = 0, l = ps.length; i < l; i++) {
                            position = ps[i];
                            posObj = result.item(position);
                            if (!posObj || posObj.hasErr) {
                                noads.push(position);
                            }
                        }

                        // handle mutual exclusion for client side fetched ads
                        if (eventId === LB_EVENT || eventId === AUTO_EVENT) {
                            for (position in MUTEX_ADS) {
                                if (MUTEX_ADS.hasOwnProperty(position) && ps.indexOf(position) >= 0 && noads.indexOf(position) === -1) {
                                    for (i = 0, l = MUTEX_ADS[position].length; i < l; i++) {
                                        mutexPos = MUTEX_ADS[position][i];
                                        if (ps.indexOf(mutexPos) >= 0 && noads.indexOf(mutexPos) === -1) {
                                            noads.push(mutexPos);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0, l = ps.length; i < l; i++) {
                                position = ps[i];
                                posName = re.exec(position)[1];
                                container = Y.one('.yom-ad-'+posName);
                                if (container) {
                                    display = container.getStyle('display');
                                    if (display === 'none' && noads.indexOf(position) === -1) {
                                        container.show();
                                    } else if (display !== 'none' && noads.indexOf(position) >= 0) {
                                        container.hide();
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    
                        // reset the hight of the LDRB container
                        if (ps.indexOf('LDRB') >= 0 && result.item('LDRB')) {
                            
                            if (noads.indexOf('LDRB') <= 0){
                                var clearAdModule = Y.one('#yom-ad-LDRB');
                                if (result.item('LDRB').size + '' !== '1x1') {
                                    clearAdModule.setStyle('height', '');
                                    Y.log('LDRB height is reset to blank.', 'info', 'darla');
                                } else {
                                    clearAdModule.setStyle('height', '5px');
                                    Y.log('LDRB height is reset to 5px.', 'info', 'darla');
                                }
                            } else {
                                Y.log('LDRB is noad or size is 1x1', 'info', 'darla');
                            }
                        }                    
                    }                    /* preparing the Nodes with iframes. Note this would be hidden iframe and not visible in the DOM */

                        return {
                            _prepareNodes: function() {
                                for(var cleanId in nodes){
                                    var center = Y.one("#"+cleanId+" > center");
                                    if(center != null && center && !Y.one("#" + nodes[cleanId].id)){
                                        center.set("innerHTML","");
                                        center.insert(nodes[cleanId].node);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        };
                    })();

                    /* setting up DARLA events */
                    var w = window,
                        D = w.DARLA,
                        C = w.DARLA_CONFIG,
                        DM = w.DOC_DOMAIN_SET || 0;
                    if (D) {
                        if (D && C) {
                            C.dm = DM;
                        }
                        
                        DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                        
                        /* setting DARLA configuration */
                        DARLA.config(C);

                        /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                        DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                        /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                        DARLA.render();  
                    }

                    return {
                        event: function (eventId, spaceId, adsSa) {
                            if (window.DARLA && eventId) {
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                                var eventConfig = {};
                                if (!isNaN(spaceId)) {
                                    eventConfig.sp = spaceId;
                                }
                                /* Site attributes */
                                adsSa = (typeof adsSa !== "undefined" && adsSa !== null) ? adsSa : "";
                                eventConfig.sa = DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace ? DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace("ADSSA", adsSa) : "";
                                DARLA.event(eventId, eventConfig);
                            }
                        },
                        render: function() {
                            if (!!(Y.one('#yom-slideshow-lightbox') || Y.one('#content-lightbox') || false)) {
                                /* skip configuring DARLA in case of lightbox being triggered */
                            } else {
                                // abort current darla action
                                if (DARLA && DARLA.abort) {
                                    DARLA.abort();
                                }

                                /* prepare node is mainly for injected ad, eg. LREC within story body */
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();

                                /* setting DARLA configuration */
                                DARLA.config(DARLA_CONFIG);

                                /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                                DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                                /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                                DARLA.render();  
                            }
                        }
                    };

     <!-- Main hero unit for a primary marketing message or call to action --> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header"> Our Mission </h1> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span8 dotted-top" role="main"> 
       <!--
                      <h2>Our Mission</h2>
        --> 
       <div class="hero-unit"> 
        <p>The Office of the President is the systemwide headquarters of the University of California.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <p>Together with the university’s executive leadership, the Office of the President helps give shape to a vision for the university, managing the activities that are central to UC's public mission and essential to the idea of one university.</p> 
         <p>Our employees manage multibillion-dollar fiscal and business operations with a clear focus on strengthening the financial health of the whole system. They establish policy frameworks that guide how UC’s academic and research missions are carried out across a complex network of campuses, labs, medical centers and community outreach programs.&nbsp;They work to ensure legal and ethical compliance, manage risk and support the health and well-being of the university's diverse workforce. They promote the university’s interests and fight for its future in Sacramento and Washington, D.C.</p> 
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <p>At the request of state policymakers, they conduct research and analysis of policies with the potential to affect all Californians. They oversee a medical enterprise that provides critical care and jobs for thousands of Californians.&nbsp;And on behalf of campuses, they lead initiatives to find smarter, more effective ways of working together to leverage the power of California’s premier university system.</p> 
         <p>Much of this work happens behind the scenes; in all of it, every day, we strive to be more efficient, decisive, responsive and transparent as we steward the amazing public resource that’s been entrusted to us.</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 sidebar"> 
       <div class="row"> 
        <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
         <h5>UC's SHARED GOVERNANCE</h5> 
         <div class="dotted-bottom"> 
          <h6>Board of Regents</h6> 
          <p>The University of California is governed by a 26-member Board of Regents that exercises approval over university policies, financial affairs, tuition and fees.</p> 
          <p><a href="http://regents.universityofcalifornia.edu">regents.universityofcalifornia.edu</a></p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="dotted-bottom"> 
          <h6>Academic Senate</h6> 
          <p>The Academic Senate represents university faculty and is empowered by the Regents to decide academic policies, including approving courses and setting requirements for admission, certificates and degrees.</p> 
          <p><a href="http://www.universityofcalifornia.edu/senate">www.universityofcalifornia.edu/senate</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span6 grybx"> 
       <h4>We want your feedback</h4> 
       <p>Find a broken link? Having trouble finding something? Submit comments, questions and feedback about the new site to our web team.</p> 
       <p><a href="mailto:webeditor@ucop.edu" title="Email us">Share feedback</a></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span6 grybx"> 
       <h4>Become an Advocate</h4> 
       <p><a href="http://www.uc4ca.org/"><img align="left" alt="UC for California logo" height="53" src="/_common/files/img/uc4ca-button.jpg" style="margin: 0px 15px 10px 0px;" width="100" /></a>Learn about events, initiatives and resources that will help you support the future of UC.</p> 
       <p><a href="http://www.uc4ca.org">Get involved</a></p> 
      </div> 
     </div>

     <ul class="posts"> 
      <li> <h2>We’ve been acquired by CloudFlare</h2> 
       <div class="wysiwyg clearfix"> 
        <div class="addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style "> 
         <a class="addthis_button_facebook_like" fb:like:layout="button_count"></a> 
         <a class="addthis_button_tweet"></a> 
         <a class="addthis_button_google_plusone" g:plusone:size="medium"></a> 
         <a class="addthis_counter addthis_pill_style"></a> 
        </div> 
        <p>Published by Dr. Anirban Banerjee</p> 
        <p>After 4 years, I’m pleased to announce that we’ve been acquired by <a href="http://www.cloudflare.com/">CloudFlare</a>, the website security and performance company.</p> 
        <p>Our mission at StopTheHacker has always been to make website security dead simple for our customers. This acquisition brings end-to-end security to CloudFlare and enables StopTheHacker to benefit from CloudFlare’s global scale. We’re evaluating how best to merge our technologies and will share more details in the future.</p> 
        <p>Rest assured, StopTheHacker will continue to work as it always has. We will continue to develop the StopTheHacker product line – in fact we just launched our <a href="https://panel.stopthehacker.com/login?loc=ja" target="_blank">Japanese version</a> last week! Nothing changes with our current partnerships with <a href="https://www.globalsign.com/">GlobalSign</a>, <a href="http://www.dreamhost.com/">DreamHost</a>, <a href="http://www.parallels.com/">Parallels</a>, <a href="http://hosteurope.co/">Host Europe</a>, <a href="http://www.verio.com/">Verio</a> or others. StopTheHacker will continue to be sold as a stand-alone product with a focus on bringing new customers and partners to our service.</p> 
        <p>The entire StopTheHacker development team is joining CloudFlare. Our head of sales, Ridley Ruth, will stay on board as our general manager responsible for sales and marketing. For sales questions, please reach out to <a href="mailto:sales@stopthehacker.com">sales@stopthehacker.com</a>.</p> 
        <p>We want to thank <a href="http://runacap.com/">Runa Capital</a> and the <a href="http://www.nsf.gov/">US National Science Foundation</a>. Without their early support, we would not have been able to grow as we did.</p> 
        <p>Most especially, we want to thank you, our customers, for your support over the years. You’ve been amazing and we hope to continue to earn your business as part of CloudFlare.</p> 
        <!-- Start Sociable -->
